function init() {
    const bcr = function (bcs, bct) {
        return bq(bcs - '0x143', bct);
    };
    const bcu = function (bcv, bcw) {
        return bw(bcv - '0x143', bcw);
    };
    const bcx = function (bcy, bcz) {
        return bq(bcy - '0x143', bcz);
    };
    const bda = function (bdb, bdc) {
        return bm(bdb - '0x143', bdc);
    };
    const bdd = function (bde, bdf) {
        return bq(bde - '0x143', bdf);
    };
    bdg[bcr('0x433')] = bcu('0x903') + bcu('0xa17') + bcu('0xcad');
    bdg[bdd('0x4ee')] = function (bdh, bdi, bdj) {
        return bdh(bdi, bdj);
    };
    bdg[bcx('0xba4')] = bdd('0x6a6') + bcr('0xa13');
    bdg[bda('0x45d')] = function (bdk, bdl) {
        return bdk(bdl);
    };
    bdg[bcu('0xb54')] = bcx('0x659') + 'o';
    bdg[bda('0xa71')] = function (bdm, bdn) {
        return bdm(bdn);
    };
    bdg[bcu('0xc2e')] = bcx('0x8b5');
    bdg[bcx('0x4ec')] = bcx('0xad5');
    bdg[bdd('0x716')] = bcu('0xc0d') + bdd('0x971') + bcr('0xbde') + bcu('0x5fa') + bcx('0xb95') + bcx('0x418') + bcr('0xc9a') + bda('0x8f6') + bda('0x8bf') + bcu('0x644') + bdd('0x415') + bdd('0xca5') + bcu('0x8c1') + bdd('0xbb3') + bcr('0x8ef') + bda('0x793');
    bdg[bdd('0x5c8')] = function (bdo, bdp) {
        return bdo(bdp);
    };
    bdg[bda('0x70e')] = bda('0xb12');
    bdg[bcr('0x683')] = bdd('0xcaa') + 'ar';
    bdg[bcr('0x522')] = bda('0x76c') + bcx('0x83f') + 'n';
    const bdq = bdr[bdd('0x433')][bdd('0x55f')]('|');
    let bds = 0;
    while (true) {
        switch (bdq[bds++]) {
        case '0':
            canbuy = false;
            continue;
        case '1':
            bdr[bcu('0x4ee')](showMenu, bdr[bdd('0xba4')], Bennys);
            continue;
        case '2':
            bdr[bcx('0x45d')]($, bdr[bcx('0xb54')])[bda('0x404')]('0');
            continue;
        case '3':
            bdr[bcx('0xa71')]($, bdr[bdd('0xc2e')])[bda('0x95e')]();
            continue;
        case '4':
            actionContainer[bdd('0x774') + bcu('0x96f')](500);
            continue;
        case '5':
            bdr[bcu('0xa71')]($, bdr[bda('0x4ec')])[bcr('0x404')](bdr[bdd('0x716')]);
            continue;
        case '6':
            bdr[bcu('0x5c8')]($, bdr[bda('0x70e')])[bda('0xace')]();
            continue;
        case '7':
            bdr[bcr('0x5c8')]($, bdr[bda('0x683')])[bdd('0xd3e')](bdr[bcx('0x522')], bdr[bda('0xba4')]);
            continue;
        }
        break;
    }
}

function showMenu(bgb, bgc) {
    const bgd = function (bge, bgf) {

    };

    };

    };

function resetWheelType() {
    const gbk = function (gbl, gbm) {
        return bq(gbl - -'0x212', gbm);
    };
    const gbn = function (gbo, gbp) {
        return bq(gbo - -'0x212', gbp);
    };
    const gbq = function (gbr, gbs) {
        return bz(gbr - -'0x212', gbs);
    };
    const gbt = function (gbu, gbv) {
        return bt(gbu - -'0x212', gbv);
    };
    const gbw = function (gbx, gby) {
        return bw(gbx - -'0x212', gby);
    };
    gbz[gbk('0x8c0')] = function (gca) {

        return gcb < gcc;
    };

        return gcd !== gce;
    };

    gbz[gbn('0x6e2')] = function (gcf, gcg) {
        return gcf != gcg;
    };
    gbz[gbq('0x9e')] = gbn('0x104') + gbn('0x3c2');
    gbz[gbt('0xa1d')] = function (gch, gci) {
        return gch !== gci;
    };
    gbz[gbn('0x5f9')] = gbt('0x207');
    gbz[gbq('0x6fa')] = gbn('0xa52');
    for (i = 0; gcj[gbk('0x7e0')](i, wheeltypes[gbk('0xa56') + 'h']); i++) {
        if (gcj[gbq('0x95b')](gcj[gbt('0x5aa')], gcj[gbt('0x965')])) {
            if (vehicle[wheeltypes[i][gbt('0x478')]] && gcj[gbw('0x6e2')](wheeltypes[i][gbw('0x478')], gcj[gbw('0x9e')])) {

                    vehicle[wheeltypes[i][gbt('0x478')]][0] = false;
                } else {
                    function gck() {
                        const gcl = gcm ? function () {
                            const gcn = function (gco, gcp) {
                                return bi(gco - -'0x2f0', gcp);
                            };
                            if (gcq) {
                                const gcr = gcs[gcn(-'0x1bf')](gct, arguments);
                                gcu = null;
                                return gcr;
                            }
                        } : function () {
                        };
                        gcv = false;
                        return gcl;
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            function gcw() {
                const gcx = function (gcy, gcz) {
                    return gbt(gcy - -'0x2e7', gcz);
                };
                const gda = function (gdb, gdc) {
                    return gbq(gdb - -'0x2e7', gdc);
                };
                const gdd = function (gde, gdf) {
                    return gbt(gde - -'0x2e7', gdf);
                };
                const gdg = function (gdh, gdi) {
                    return gbw(gdh - -'0x2e7', gdi);
                };
                const gdj = function (gdk, gdl) {
                    return gbq(gdk - -'0x2e7', gdl);
                };

                gdn[gda('0x126')](gcj[gcx('0x1c9')], gdo[gcx('0x341') + gcx('0x234')]({ type: gcj[gda(-'0x229')] }));
            }
        }
    }
    return false;
}
function changeColor(gdp) {
    const gdq = function (gdr, gds) {
        return bq(gdr - '0x78', gds);
    };
    const gdt = function (gdu, gdv) {
        return bz(gdu - '0x78', gdv);
    };
    const gdw = function (gdx, gdy) {
        return bt(gdx - '0x78', gdy);
    };
    const gdz = function (gea, geb) {
        return bq(gea - '0x78', geb);
    };
    const gec = function (ged, gee) {
        return bm(ged - '0x78', gee);
    };
    gef[gdq('0xc12')] = function (geg, geh) {
        return geg(geh);
    };
    gef[gdq('0x7e9')] = function (gei, gej) {
        return gei + gej;
    };
    gef[gdw('0x90e')] = function (gek, gel) {
        return gek(gel);
    };
    gef[gdz('0x397')] = gdz('0x8b4') + gdq('0x562') + 'e';
    gef[gdw('0x938')] = gdq('0x585') + gdw('0xa16') + gdz('0x934') + gdw('0x3f4') + gdw('0x621') + gdw('0x3b3') + gdz('0x79d') + gec('0xb6b') + ' ';
    gef[gdw('0x552')] = gec('0x39e') + gdz('0xa8a') + gdw('0x9a4') + gdt('0xa96') + gec('0x3f5') + ')';
    gef[gdz('0x61f')] = gdt('0x8b4') + 'r';
    gef[gdz('0x7f1')] = gec('0x606') + gec('0x4be');
    gef[gec('0x517')] = gdt('0x629') + gec('0xc80') + gdz('0x488') + gdt('0x6e4') + gdw('0x9a9') + gdw('0x84e');
    gef[gdt('0x812')] = function (gem, gen) {
        return gem(gen);
    };
    let geo = gep[gec('0xc12')]($, gep[gdq('0x7e9')]('#', gdp))[gdq('0x371')]();
    gep[gdz('0x90e')]($, gep[gdq('0x397')])[gdw('0x339')](geo);
    let geq = gep[gdz('0x7e9')](gep[gdw('0x7e9')](gep[gec('0x938')], geo), gep[gdt('0x552')]);
    gep[gec('0x90e')]($, gep[gec('0x61f')])[gec('0x56d')](gep[gdz('0x7f1')], geq);
    $[gdz('0x697')](gep[gec('0x517')], JSON[gdq('0x8b2') + gdq('0x7a5')]({
        type: gdp,
        color: gep[gdz('0x812')](toRGB, geo)
    }));
    vehicle[gdp] = geo;
}
function toRGB(ger) {
    const ges = function (get, geu) {
        return bz(get - -'0x2dc', geu);
    };
    const gev = function (gew, gex) {
        return bq(gew - -'0x2dc', gex);
    };
    const gey = function (gez, gfa) {
        return bt(gez - -'0x2dc', gfa);
    };
    const gfb = function (gfc, gfd) {
        return bt(gfc - -'0x2dc', gfd);
    };
    const gfe = function (gff, gfg) {
        return bm(gff - -'0x2dc', gfg);
    };
    gfh[ges('0x621')] = gev('0x2d5') + ges('0x92c') + gev('0x134') + gfb('0x390') + gey('0x655') + ges('0x4fa');
    gfh[ges('0x271')] = function (gfi, gfj) {
        return gfi === gfj;
    };
    gfh[ges('0x81d')] = ges('0x5cc');
    gfh[gfe(-'0xe')] = function (gfk, gfl, gfm) {
        return gfk(gfl, gfm);
    };
    let gfn = ger[ges('0x1a7')](/[A-Za-z0-9]{2}/g)[ges('0x919')](function (gfo) {
        const gfp = function (gfq, gfr) {
            return gev(gfq - -'0x187', gfr);
        };
        const gfs = function (gft, gfu) {
            return gfe(gft - -'0x187', gfu);
        };
        const gfv = function (gfw, gfx) {
            return gfe(gfw - -'0x187', gfx);
        };
        const gfy = function (gfz, gga) {
            return gfe(gfz - -'0x187', gga);
        };
        if (ggb[gfp('0xea')](ggb[gfp('0x696')], ggb[gfv('0x696')])) {
            return ggb[gfy(-'0x195')](parseInt, gfo, 16);
        } else {
            function ggc() {
                const ggd = function (gge, ggf) {
                    return gfp(gge - -'0x10f', ggf);
                };
                const ggg = function (ggh, ggi) {
                    return gfs(ggh - -'0x10f', ggi);
                };
                const ggj = function (ggk, ggl) {
                    return gfv(ggk - -'0x10f', ggl);
                };
                const ggm = function (ggn, ggo) {
                    return gfy(ggn - -'0x10f', ggo);
                };
                const ggp = function (ggq, ggr) {
                    return gfs(ggq - -'0x10f', ggr);
                };
                ggs[ggt] = true;
                ggu[ggd('0x4e4')] = this.id;
                ggv[ggd('0xad')](ggb[ggj('0x38b')], ggw[ggm('0x2c8') + ggd('0x1bb')](ggu));
            }
        }
    })[gey('0x49')](',');
    return gfn;
}
